[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePath[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:177[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:86[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:460[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:400[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:324[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:204[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based security check reported a critical file path traversal issue during [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz testing of the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example. The sanitizer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected that a constructed path [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m…[0m[35m/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m escapes the intended [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction directory. The exception originates from the FilePathTraversal sanitizer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand surfaces when the fuzzer invokes `Expander.expand` via the test harness.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer triggered a [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception of type [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“File path traversal.” The sanitizer identified that the code allowed a relative [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath containing “..” segments to reach outside the designated extraction directory.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal is explicitly flagged by `FilePathTraversal.check` in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer sanitizers. This represents a critical security issue: an attacker-supplied [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath may escape an intended directory boundary.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception stack trace shows the sequence:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `FilePathTraversal.check` → `checkPath` → `pathFirstArgHook`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Then cascading calls in [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand` at lines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer’s input caused the code to resolve “..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m,” [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrating inadequate path normalization or sanitization in the extraction [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is only the entry point for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzz test and is not the root cause.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Locations for Investigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **FilePathTraversal.java** – methods `check`, `checkPath`, and [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`pathFirstArgHook` in the Jazzer sanitizers to understand how the path is validated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand where traversal is detected.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Expander.java** – the `expand` methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnotably around lines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where archive entries are written to disk. Attention should be paid to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath resolution, normalization, and how entry names are concatenated with the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **ExpanderFuzzer.java** – the fuzz harness that invokes `Expander.expand`. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhile not the fault, it maps fuzz inputs to archive data and drives coverage of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction logic.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis evaluation report focuses on the critical path traversal detection without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspeculating on underlying causes or prescribing fixes.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis and Root Cause  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The critical file path traversal arises because the default `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in `ArchiveEntry` performs URL decoding *after* an initial [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization and security check. This allows attacker-supplied percent-encoded [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..” segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `%2E%2E`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to slip past the first check, then be decoded into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreal “..” segments and escape the intended extraction directory.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All of the `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` code relies on [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to produce a safe, normalized output path. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBecause `resolveIn` can return a non-normalized path, the fuzzer sanitizer flags [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe write to disk as a traversal vulnerability.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only functionality change is to ensure decoding occurs *before* [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization and path-boundary checking.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We retain the existing API signature and the `IOException` for zip-slip [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection. The fallback behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39min case decoding fails[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains, but now also [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundergoes normalization and boundary checking.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All `Expander` code continues to call `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unmodified; no patches [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto archive-writing logic or fuzz harness are required.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplace the body of the default `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method with the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing logic:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Retrieve the raw entry name via `[0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Attempt to URL-decode it. On any decoding exception, fall back to the raw [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Resolve `[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then call `[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Perform a single `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check on the normalized path.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If it passes, return the normalized path; otherwise throw an `IOException` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mciting zip-slip.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Ensure the thrown `IOException` message remains consistent [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' +[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for compatibility.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Example Replacement Implementation  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfile: `ArchiveEntry.java`, lines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String rawName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String decodedName;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawName, [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m fall back to raw name if decoding fails[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = rawName;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Resolve and normalize after decoding[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final Path resolved = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                               parentPath, decodedName, resolved[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return resolved;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Note: This replaces the two-stage `normalize -> check -> decode -> return` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequence with a single consistent decode-then-normalize flow.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Mitigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By moving URL decoding *before* normalization and path boundary checking, any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoded “..” segments are expanded then sanitized, closing the traversal gap.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalization ensures removal of redundant separators and “.”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“..” segments so[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check is reliable.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If decoding fails, falling back to the raw name still normalizes and checks [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly, preserving robustness against malformed input.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other parts of the codebase are touched, so existing tests and CI [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding fuzz harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unaffected.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add or update unit tests to cover percent-encoded traversal names such as [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“%2E%2E/evil.txt” to assert that `resolveIn` throws `IOException`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run existing archive-extraction example tests against valid entries to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm behavior is unchanged.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm by re-running the Jazzer fuzz job that `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno longer flags this scenario in `Expander.expand`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache Commons Compress codebase triggered a       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         critical security exception for file path traversal. The exception originated when  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.expand` attempted to write output files with traversing paths [1m([0me.g.       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”[1m)[0m. In response, a patch was proposed to harden              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath[1m)[0m` by URL-decoding the entry name, normalizing the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         result, and re-checking that the resolved path stays within the parent directory.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         After applying the patch, the Maven build failed with a compilation error in        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ArchiveEntry.java`, reporting that the variable `decodedName` “might already have  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         been assigned.”                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Initial Issue                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Exception:                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           at [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           at                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           at [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           at [1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Symptoms:                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The fuzzer input caused `Expander` to write paths that include “..[35m/[0m[95m..[0m”, leading   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer to raise a security exception.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Observations:                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The failure occurs during fuzzing of archive expansion.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The stack trace points to `pathFirstArgHook` intercepting file-opening calls    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with a dangerous path.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The archive‐entry resolution logic had only a simple “zip-slip” check, and the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         patch attempt sought to tighten it.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Patch Attempt                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         In `org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, the default           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         implementation of                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             default Path [1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mfinal Path parentPath[1m)[0m throws IOException                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was replaced. The original code:                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final String name = [1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final Path outputFile = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             if [1m([0m![1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                     [1;35mString.format[0m[1m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m,                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                   parentPath, name, outputFile[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             try [1m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 return [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                     [1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname, [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m catch [1m([0mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[1m)[0m [1m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 return outputFile;                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was changed to:                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final String rawName = [1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final String decodedName;                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             try [1m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 decodedName = [1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mrawName,                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                 [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m catch [1m([0mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[1m)[0m [1m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 decodedName = rawName;                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final Path resolved = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             if [1m([0m![1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                     [1;35mString.format[0m[1m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m,                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                   parentPath, decodedName, resolved[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             return resolved;                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This rewrite aims to:                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. URL-decode the entry name once, falling back to the raw name on error.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Normalize the resulting path.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Enforce the same “startsWith” parent directory check before returning.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Result of Applying the Patch                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         When rebuilding with Maven:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         – The compiler error occurs in `ArchiveEntry.java` at the line declaring or         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         assigning `decodedName`:                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           `[1m[[0mERROR[1m][0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiveEn[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mtry.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m84[0m,[1;36m13[0m[1m][0m variable decodedName might already have been assigned`             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         – The build stops with a “BUILD FAILURE” and no further compilation of fuzzers      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         proceeds.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Further Investigation                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         should be examined:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath[1m)[0m**                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            – Potential interactions between the sanitizer’s logic and the code in           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Reviewing these areas will help understand both the root of the traversal           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:                final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:            nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Required Change[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The proposed security fix correctly moves URL-decoding before normalization [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the “startsWith” check but declared `decodedName` as a `final` variable without[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man initializer. Java’s definite-assignment rules then flag “variable decodedName [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmight already have been assigned.”[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To both resolve the compile error and preserve the security hardening, we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Initialize `decodedName` in its declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso it’s always assigned once[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Remove the `final` modifier [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor keep it on variables with single assignment[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpost‐initialization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Decode into that mutable variable inside a try/catch.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d. Normalize and check the decoded result.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` default method:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the uninitialized `final String decodedName;` with a single [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration and initialization:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String decodedName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Decode inside a try/catch, reassigning into the same variable:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName, [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException ignored[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m fallback stays as raw name[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Resolve, normalize, and enforce the zip-slip check:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path resolved = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                            parentPath, decodedName, resolved[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return resolved;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Remove any prior `outputFile` variable and the old decode-after-normalize [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode path.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method still:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. URL-decodes entry names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalling back on raw names on decoding errors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Normalizes the decoded path.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Throws an `IOException` on any attempt to escape the `parentPath` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mprotecting against both raw and percent-encoded “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” attacks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., format-specific entries or the fuzzer harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified. Existing tests and the fuzzer will exercise this code in the same way, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow with the strengthened guard.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Decoding/normalization occur exactly once per entry; performance impact is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exception message and type remain unchanged for zip-slip violations, so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many logging or monitoring relying on those messages will continue to function.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Because we removed `final` on `decodedName`, there’s no semantic change other [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan satisfying the compiler.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No Harness or Test Code Changes[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness continues to call `resolveIn` unchanged.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests need updating since only illegal inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthose with traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreliably throw before writing.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
